NOTIFICATIONS BY GOVERNMENT
HIGHWAYS AND MINOR PORTS DEPARTMENT
Acquisition of Lands
Amendment to Notiﬁ cation
[G.O. (D) No.27, Highways and Minor Ports (HF2), 
9th February 2022, ¬î 27, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HWMP/121/2022.—The following Amendment 
is issued to G.O. (D) No.111, Highways and Minor Port 
(HF2) Department, dated 12.08.2020 and the Notiﬁ cation 
No.II(2)/HW&MP/497/2020 published at pages 606-610 of 
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette No.33, Part II—Section 2, 
dated 12.08.2020. 
Aඕඍඖඌඕඍඖග
In the Appendix Notiﬁ cation of G.O. (D) No. 111, Highways 
and Minor Ports (HF2) Department, dated 12.08.2020 under 
the heading SCHEDULE Tiruvallur District, Ponneri Taluk, 
Vijayanallur Village for the existing details in the Serial 
No.65, the following details shall be substituted.
SI.
No.
Read as
65
Government Dry Land in S.No.14 / 2A now 
sub divided as 14 / 2A1A1A2 belonging to Mini, 
W/o. Chandran-1, R.Kandhan-2, T.Parthasarathy-3, 
T.S. Parthasarathy-4, Rajeshkumar Mundra-5, 
V.P. Muthaiya Rajan-6, A.Muniammal-7, 
P.Jayachandran-8, B.Saroja-9, K.Vijayakumar-10, 
bounded on the North by No.114 Nallur Village, 
S.No.14/1, S.No.14/3, S.No.14/2C, S.No.14/5,
S.No.14/2A1A1A1, East by S.No.14/1, S.No.14/3, 
S.No.14/2C, S.No.14/5, S.No.13, South by 
S.No.14/3, S.No.14/2B, S.No.14/2C, S.No.14/5, 
S.No.13, S.No.15 and West by S.No.14/2A1A1A1, 
S.No.14/2C, S.No.14/5 — 4874 Sq.mts.
Government Dry Land in S.No.14/2A 
now sub divided as 14/2C belonging to 
E. Elizabeth, W/o. R. Eraliyan–bounded on the 
North by S.No.14/2A1A1A2, East by 14/2A1A1A2, 
South by S.No.14/2A1A1A2 and West by 
S.No.14/2A1A1A2 --- 150 Sq.mts.
 
 
 
 
 
DHEERAJ KUMAR,
  
 
 
 
 Principal Secretary to Government.
HIGHER EDUCATION DEPARTMENT
Nomination of Member to the Academic Committee 
of Mother Teresa Women's University, Kodaikanal 
under the Mother Teresa Women's University Act, 1984.
[G.O. (D) No. 34, Higher Education (K1), 15th February 2022, 
ñ£C 3, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HE/122/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred under clause (4) of Class II-Other Members of 
Section 20 under Chapter III of Mother Teresa Women's 
University Act, 1984, the Government hereby nominate 
Dr. K.S. Pushpa, Professor of Home Science Extension, 
Gandhigram Rural University, Coimbatore as member 
to the Academic Committee of Mother Teresa Women's 
University, Kodaikanal, for a period of three years with 
eﬀ ect from the date of issue of this order.
 
 
 
 
D. KARTHIKEYAN,
 
 
          Principal Secretary to Government.
HOME DEPARTMENT
Constitution of a Sub Court at Polur in Tiruvannamalai 
District under the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 72,  Home (Courts-III), 11th February 2022, 
¬î 29, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HO/123/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by the ﬁ rst paragraph of Section 4 of the 
Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act, 1873 (Central Act III  of 1873), 
the Governor of Tamil Nadu, hereby alters the number of 
Subordinate Judges to be appointed under the said Act for 
Tiruvannamalai District as SEVEN with eﬀ ect from the date 
on which the Subordinate Judge, assumes charge of the 
Subordinate Judge's Court at Polur.
NOTIFICATION-II
[G.O. Ms. No. 72,  Home (Courts-III), 11th February 2022, 
¬î 29, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HO/124/2022.—In 
exercise 
of 
the 
powers 
Conferred by the second paragraph of Section 4 of the 
Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873), 
the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consultation with the 
High Court, Madras hereby ﬁ xes the number of Subordinate 
Judges to be appointed for the Subordinate Judge's Court 
at Polur in Tiruvannamalai District as ONE with eﬀ ect from 
the date on which the Subordinate Judge, Polur assumes 
charge of that Court.
NOTIFICATION-III
[G.O. Ms. No. 72,  Home (Courts-III), 11th February 2022, 
¬î 29, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HO/125/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by Section 5 of the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts 
Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu, hereby ﬁ xes Polur in Tiruvannamalai   District 
as the place at which the Subordinate Judge’s Court, 
Polur shall be held.
NOTIFICATION-IV
[G.O. Ms. No. 72,  Home (Courts-III), 11th February 2022, 
¬î 29, Hôõ, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2053.]
No.II(2)/HO/126/2022.—In exercise of the powers 
conferred by Section 10 of the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts 
Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873), the Governor of 
Tamil Nadu, hereby directs that in the District of 
Tiruvannamalai, the Subordinate Judge’s Court at Arni 
shall cease to have original jurisdiction over the District 
Munsif Court, Polur and the Sub Court, Tiruvannamalai 
shall cease to  have local Jurisdiction over the local limits 
of the District Munsif-cum-Judicial Magistrate Court, 
Kalasapakkam and hereby ﬁ xes the Local Limits of the 
District Munsif Court, Polur and the District Munsif-cum-
Judicial Magistrate Court, Kalasapakkam as the local Limits 
of jurisdiction of the Subordinate Judge’s Court at Polur 
with eﬀ ect from the date on which the Subordinate 
Judge, Polur assumes charge of that Court.
                                                        S.K. PRABAKAR,
                                Additional Chief Secretary to Government.


Mar. 2, 2022]

Declaration of Nadugani Kunnu Addition Forest Block 
in Gudalur Taluk, The Nilgiris District as Reserved 
Forest under the Tamil Nadu Forest Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 58, Environment, Climate Change-Forest (FR.14), 
27th  August 2021, ÝõE 
11, 
Hôõ, 
F¼õœÀõ˜ 
Ý‡´-2052.]
No.II(2)/ECCF/133/2022.— In exercise of the powers 
conferred by section 16-A of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 
(Tamil Nadu Act V of 1882), the Governor of Tamil Nadu 
hereby declares the land vested with the Government under 
the Gudalur Janmam Estates  (Abolition and Conversion into 
Ryotwari Act, 1969 (Tamil Nadu Act 24 of 1969) and already 
determined as forest by the Settlement Oﬃ  cer under the said 
Act, the area and boundaries of which are specﬁ ed in the 
Schedule below, as reserved forest.

:

:

:

Village

Forest block
:

:

acres
BOUNDARIES.
Survey Number 147/4.
North:-The boundary line starts from the tri-junction of 
Survey Numbers 150, 148 and 147/4 of Devala Village, the 
boundary generally runs southeastwards along the southern 
boundary of Survey Number 148 of Devala Village and 
meets at the tri-junction of Survey Numbers 148, 147/1 
and 147/4 of Devala Village.
East:-Thence, the boundary generally runs southwest 
wards, southwards and southeastwards along the western 
and southern boundary of Survey Number 147/1 and meets 
at the tri-junction point of Survey Numbers 147/1, 185 and 
147/4 of Devala Village. Then the boundary generally runs 
southwards along the western portion of Survey Number 
185 of Devala Village and meets at the junction of Survey 
Number 185 and 147/4 of Devala Village.
South:-Thence, the boundary generally runs westwards 
along the northern portion of Survey Number 185 of Devala 
Village and meets at the tri-junction of Survey Numbers 
185, 147/3 and 147/4 of Devala Village. 
West:-Thence, the boundary generally runs northwards 
along the eastern portion of Survey Number 147/3, 145 
and 150 of Devala Village till it reaches the starting 
point. 
Survey Number 147/5.
North:-Starting from the bi-junction of Survey Numbers 
147/1 and 147/5 of Devala Village, the boundary generally 
runs northeastwards to a distance of 90.40 metres along 
the southeast portion of Survey Number 147/1 of Devala 
Village and meets at tri-junction of Survey Numbers 147/1, 
185 and 147/5 of Devala Village.
East:-Thence, the boundary generally runs southwards 
along the western portion of Survey Numbers 185 and 
147/1 of Devala Village and meets at the bi-junction point 
of Survey Numbers 147/1 and 147/5 of Devala Village.
South and West:-Thence, the boundary generally runs 
northwestwards and northwards along the eastern portion 
of Survey Number 147/1 of Devala Village and meets at 
the starting point.
 
SUPRIYA SAHU, 
 
 
Principal Secretary to Government.
